country_event = {
    id = 836592378
    title = "The Fate of Malaysia"
    desc = "MALAYSIAFATE"
    picture = "malaysia_fate"
    is_triggered_only = yes

    option = {
        name = "We simply aim to unify the administration of the Malay peninsula."
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = JOH
				OR = {
					in_sphere = THIS
					vassal_of = THIS
				}
			}
			annex_to = THIS
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = PHG
				OR = {
					in_sphere = THIS
					vassal_of = THIS
				}
			}
			annex_to = THIS
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = PRK
				OR = {
					in_sphere = THIS
					vassal_of = THIS
				}
			}
			annex_to = THIS
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = SLG
				OR = {
					in_sphere = THIS
					vassal_of = THIS
				}
			}
			annex_to = THIS
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = JOH }
				any_owned_province = { is_core = JOH }
				OR = {
					in_sphere = THIS
					vassal_of = THIS
				}
			}
			any_owned = {
				limit = { is_core = JOH }
				secede_province = THIS
			}
		}
		JOH = {
			all_core = {
				remove_core = JOH
			}
		}
		SLG = {
			all_core = {
				remove_core = SLG
			}
		}
		PHG = {
			all_core = {
				remove_core = PHG
			}
		}
		PRK = {
			all_core = {
				remove_core = PRK
			}
		}
		ENG_1384 = { add_core = MLY }
		ENG_1391 = { add_core = MLY }
		any_owned = {
			limit = {
				is_core = MLY
				is_core = THIS
			}
			remove_core = MLY
		}
		any_pop = {
			limit = { has_pop_culture = malay }
			militancy = -6
		}
		1388 = { remove_core = MLY }
		1386 = { remove_core = MLY }
		1384 = { remove_core = MLY }
		release_vassal = MLY
		1388 = { add_core = MLY }
		1386 = { add_core = MLY }
		1384 = { add_core = MLY }
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
    }

    option = {
        name = "The new Malaysian state shall have the goal of uniting the region!"
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = JOH
				OR = {
					in_sphere = THIS
					vassal_of = THIS
				}
			}
			annex_to = THIS
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = PHG
				OR = {
					in_sphere = THIS
					vassal_of = THIS
				}
			}
			annex_to = THIS
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = PRK
				OR = {
					in_sphere = THIS
					vassal_of = THIS
				}
			}
			annex_to = THIS
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = SLG
				OR = {
					in_sphere = THIS
					vassal_of = THIS
				}
			}
			annex_to = THIS

		}
		NET_1426 = { add_core = MLY }
		BRU_1395 = { add_core = MLY }
		BRU_1394 = { add_core = MLY }

    id = 836592377
    title = "Unification with Romania"
    desc = "TINYROMANIANSTRIP"
    picture = "tiny_moldavia"

    trigger = {
		primary_culture = romanian
		war = no
		is_vassal = no
		neighbour = ROM
		owns = 673
		owns = 678
		NOT = {
			owns = 677
			owns = 676
			owns = 670
			owns = 668
			owns = 675
			owns = 3372
			owns = 968
			owns = 969
			owns = 814
			owns = 795
			owns = 653
			owns = 659
			owns = 660
		}
    }

    mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }

    option = {
        name = "The time has come to rejoin what was once wrought asunder!"
		ROM = { inherit = THIS }
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
    }

    option = {
        name = "Never! We will maintain our independence forever."
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
    }
}

country_event = {
    id = 836592376
    title = "$COUNTRY_ADJ$ Egypt"
    desc = "Now that we have conquered Egypt, the time has come to impose a colonial administration on it."
    picture = "cairo"
    fire_only_once = yes

    trigger = {
		has_global_flag = egypt_was_civ
		owns = 1745
		NOT = { tag = EGY primary_culture = misri }
    }

    mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }

    option = {
        name = "Huzzah!"
		any_owned = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core = EGY
					is_core = SUD
				}
			}
			secede_province = UTI
		}
		inherit = UTI
    }
}

country_event = {
    id = 9275639
    title = "Monarchy Government Flag Setup"
    desc = "This is apparently necessary."
    picture = "walter"
    is_triggered_only = yes

    option = {
        name = "Das schönste Land in Deutschlands Gaun, das ist das Badnerland!"
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					government = hms_government
					government = prussian_constitutionalism
					government = absolute_monarchy
					government = absolute_empire
					government = semi_constitutional_empire
					government = constitutional_empire
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = monarchy_government
		}
    }
}

    title = "The Flour Riot of 1837"
    desc = "FLOURRIOT"
    picture = "flour_riot"
    fire_only_once = yes

    trigger = {
		year = 1837
		tag = USA
		owns = 232
		month = 2
    }

    mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }

    option = {
        name = "Damn Locofocos..."
		232 = {
			any_pop = {
				ideology = { factor = 0.2 value = radical }
				scaled_consciousness = { factor = 4 ideology = radical }
				scaled_militancy = { factor = 4 ideology = radical }
				militancy = 4
				consciousness = 6
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
    }
}

country_event = {
	id = 847295
	title = "The Battle of Pákozd"
	desc = "PAKOZDBATTLE"
	picture = "pakozd"
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "Éljen Magyarország!"
		set_country_flag = hungarian_revolution_began
		small_arms = 100
		regular_clothes = 100
		define_general = { name = "Józef Bem" personality = defence_3.1 background = attack_1.1 }
		define_general = { name = "János Móga" personality = no_personality background = attack_3.1 }
		define_general = { name = "Mór Perczel" personality = defence_1.1 background = attack_1.1 }
		define_general = { name = "Artúr Görgei" personality = defence_2.1 background = attack_minus_1.1 }
		define_general = { name = "György Klapka" personality = defence_1.1 background = no_background }
		define_general = { name = "János Damjanich" personality = defence_2.1 background = attack_2.1 }
		define_general = { name = "Lajos Aulich" personality = defence_minus_1.1 background = attack_2.1 }
		define_general = { name = "Károly Vécsey" personality = no_personality background = attack_2.1 }
		define_general = { name = "András Gáspár" personality = defence_1.1 background = attack_2.1 }
		define_general = { name = "Henryk Dembinski" personality = defence_1.1 background = attack_2.1 }
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = begin_revolution
			duration = 365
		}
		any_pop = {
			limit = { has_pop_culture = hungarian }
			militancy = -8
		}
		any_owned = {
			limit = { is_core = ROM }
			any_pop = {
				limit = { has_pop_culture = romanian }
				militancy = 6
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = nationalist_agitation
				duration = 1095
			}
		}
		any_owned = {
			limit = { is_core = SER }
			any_pop = {
				limit = { has_pop_culture = serb }
				militancy = 6
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = nationalist_agitation
				duration = 1095
			}
		}
		AUS = {
			war = {
				target = HUN
				attacker_goal = {
					casus_belli = annex_core_country
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = slovaks_are_mad
		set_country_flag = serbs_are_mad
	}
}

#Cuba asks for Isla de Pinos
country_event = {
	id = 16061935
	title = "The Hay-Quesada Treaty"
	desc = "HAYQUESADA"
	picture = "hay_quesada"

    fire_only_once = yes

    trigger = {
		year = 1925
		tag = USA
		has_country_flag = cuban_occupation
		owns = 3660
		CUB = { owns = 2209 }
		NOT = { war_with = CUB truce_with = CUB }
	}

    mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }

	option = {
        name = "We must recognize the Isle of Pines as Cuban. §GLose 1 infamy§W"
		badboy = -1
		3660 = { secede_province = CUB }
		relation = { who = CUB value = 150 }
	}
	option = {
        name = "The Isle of Pines is clearly not part of Cuba."
		relation = { who = CUB value = -150 }
	}
}

#After US has won the Spanish-American War, they get event 37741 in SPAFlavor.txt
#Option 2 of 3 there lets them decide to occupy Cuba for a couple years (historical)
#This event is Cuba asking for independence in 1902
country_event = {
	id = 16061934
	title = "The Cuban Constitution"
	desc = "CUBACONST"
	picture = "estrada_palma"

    fire_only_once = yes

    trigger = {
		year = 1902
		tag = USA
		has_country_flag = cuban_occupation
		owns = 2209
		CUB = { exists = no }
	}

    mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }

	option = {
        name = "Force them to integrate the Platt Amendment. §RGain 1 infamy§!"
		badboy = 1
		release_vassal = CUB
		3660 = { secede_province = THIS }
		44 = { secede_province = THIS }
        relation = {
            who = CUB
            value = 200
        }
        diplomatic_influence = {
            who = CUB
            value = 200
        }
		CUB = {
			government = democracy
			political_reform = universal_voting
			political_reform = secret_ballots
		}
	}
	option = {
        name = "Cuba is ready for independence."
		any_owned = {
			limit = {
				is_core = CUB
			}
			secede_province = CUB
		}
		3660 = { secede_province = THIS }
		44 = { secede_province = THIS }
        relation = {
            who = CUB
            value = 200
        }
        diplomatic_influence = {
            who = CUB
            value = 200
        }
		CUB = {
			government = democracy
			political_reform = universal_voting
			political_reform = secret_ballots
		}
	}
}

# Peru-Bolivian Confederation - fires for BOL
country_event = {
	id = 16051934
	title = "The Peru-Bolivian Confederation"
	desc = "BOLIVIACONFEDERATESWPERU"

    fire_only_once = yes

    trigger = {
		tag = BOL
		PEU = { 
			vassal_of = THIS

		}

    title = "The loss of Massenya"
    desc = "Without a land connection to Massenya, the owners of Doba have taken it over."
    trigger = {
       owns = 3746
	   NOT = {
		owns = 3896
	   }
	   NOT = {
		owns = 1818
	   }
	   NOT = {
		owns = 1825
	   }
	   NOT = {
		owns = 1820
	   }
	   NOT = {
		owns = 1964
	   }
    }
    mean_time_to_happen = {
        days = 1
    }
    option = {
        name = "Tragic!"
        1818 = { owner = { country_event = 54678908 } }
    }
}

country_event = {
    id = 789678731
    title = "Moundou"
    desc = "Without a land connection to Moundou, we can no longer defend it. $FROMCOUNTRY$ will therefore take it over."
	is_triggered_only = yes
    option = {
        name = "Tragic!"
		any_owned = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					province_id = 1819
					province_id = 3929
					province_id = 1967
				}
			}
			secede_province = FROM
		}
    }
}
